# Musu-Bee Wiki ID Index

**Generated**: 2026-05-27
**Scope**: `F:\workspace\musu-bee\docs\` — all wiki-identified docs (`**Wiki ID**: wiki/N` header)
**Source of truth**: each doc's own `**Wiki ID**` header. This file is a roll-up index — when a doc and this index disagree, the doc wins.

Layout:
- §1 — Master plans (V21..V23.5)
- §2 — Sub-WS detail plans + closures + qual evals (V23.1..V23.4 Phase 4)
- §3 — V23.4 Phase 4 (current shipped — wiki/431..448)
- §4 — V23.5 (reserved — wiki/459..482)
- §4.5 — V24..V26 Rust-native / distributed actor line
- §4.6 — 1.15.0-rc.1 beta readiness line
- §5 — Research / brainstorm / architecture (wiki/449..458)
- §5.5 — Windows distribution pivot working set (2026-05-27, no wiki ID)
- §6 — Pre-V21 docs (no wiki ID; archived/legacy)
- §7 — New code files this Phase 4 (entry-point inventory, no wiki ID)

Status legend:
- `complete` — file exists, wiki ID assigned, closure phase done
- `draft` — file exists, in active iteration
- `reserved` — wiki ID reserved in a planning doc, file not yet created
- `legacy` — pre-V21, no wiki ID

The spec's D7/RV1/C11 rows were revised on 2026-05-22 to match implementation. M1 cycle (musu /goal master plan) closed W1 chokepoint; M2 (W7 `musu peer register`) is next.

2026-05-31 second-PC MSIX install operator runbook: `SECOND_PC_MSIX_INSTALL_OPERATOR_RUNBOOK_2026_05_31.md` is the focused human checklist for copying the latest operator action pack to a real second Windows PC, running `run-second-pc-release-check.ps1`, returning `.local-build\second-pc-return\*.zip`, and importing it with `import-second-pc-return.ps1 -RecordMsixInstall`. 2026-05-31 runtime hardening and relay roadmap: `RELEASE_1_15_0_RC1_RUNTIME_HARDENING_RELAY_ROADMAP_2026_05_31.md` (wiki/523) records the updated No-Go reason after second-PC MSIX evidence returned. The release is now blocked by internal runtime quality as well as external evidence: operator-observed idle CPU busy-loop behavior, missing two-machine idle CPU evidence, remaining packaged desktop/startup collision proof, source-fresh release packaging OOM/pagefile failure on HUGH_SECOND, and insufficient `musu.pro` assisted rendezvous/relay-control path. `measure-musu-idle-cpu.ps1` writes `musu.runtime_idle_cpu_evidence.v1`, `write-release-go-no-go.ps1` reports `runtime_idle_cpu_verified`, and public beta requires a running MUSU runtime process plus <=5% of one logical CPU over a 60s idle sample on at least two machines. The idle CPU sampler now uses native Windows parent-process lookup and helper scope metadata so `-IncludeNode -IncludeWebView2` counts MUSU-owned descendants or repo-related helpers by default instead of every stale machine-wide WebView2/Node process; `-IncludeUnrelatedHelpers` is diagnostic-only. `audit-musu-process-ownership.ps1` writes `musu.process_ownership_audit.v1`, `audit-musu-startup-single-instance.ps1` writes `musu.startup_single_instance_audit.v1`, and `write-release-go-no-go.ps1` reports both `process_ownership_verified` and `startup_single_instance_verified`. Universal clipboard polling is now opt-in via `MUSU_ENABLE_CLIPBOARD_SYNC=1`. Frontend polling now uses shared `useLowDutyPolling` for major idle dashboard/panel/inbox surfaces, 30s fleet/company/machine safety-net polling plus SSE wakeups, abort-on-unmount, hidden-tab pause, no overlap, and capped failure backoff. Writer task admission now uses `tokio::sync::Notify` instead of 50ms slot polling under backlog. MSIX artifact packaging now uses `musu-desktop.exe` as the app executable and passes Store bundle artifact verification; installed evidence still requires reinstall.

2026-05-31 MUSU Pro P2P control-plane spec: `MUSU_PRO_P2P_CONTROL_PLANE_SPEC_2026_05_31.md` (wiki/524) locks the next multi-device architecture: `musu.pro` is the control plane for registry, rendezvous, path selection, relay/tunnel fallback, and route evidence, not the default data path. Route kinds are `lan`, `tailscale`, `direct_quic`, `relay`, and `failed`; route evidence must record peer identity verification, handshake timing, encryption, and whether payload transited MUSU infrastructure. Core remains localhost/LAN/user-managed private routes; hosted relay/tunnel remains Connect/Pro.

2026-06-01 MUSU Pro P2P runtime update: wiki/524 now reflects that bridge runtime forwarding creates/refreshes a short-lived `musu.pro` rendezvous session before legacy direct forwarding when logged in, publishes the source endpoint, can replace the original selected peer with the best returned target candidate, falls back once to the original peer if that candidate fails, carries `rendezvous_session_id` to the target, lets the target publish candidates on receipt, closes the session after terminal success/failure, and records the session id in route evidence. Candidate updates now refresh a recent node candidate cache, and new sessions seed source/target candidates from that cache when available. `musu relay status --json` and `musu route --explain --json` now report `rendezvous_session_wired=true`. This is still not release-grade because the transport remains HTTP bearer, peer identity/QUIC-TLS proof is not wired, relay/tunnel data transport is absent, and real second-PC target-candidate evidence is missing.

2026-06-01 peer identity material update: wiki/524 and wiki/528 now reflect that MUSU carries advertised TLS certificate fingerprints through the P2P control plane. Rust can compute local cert SHA-256 fingerprints, logged-in bridge registration sends `cert_fingerprint`/`peer_public_key`, rendezvous candidates publish the fingerprint as `public_key`, refreshed target candidates carry it into route peer metadata, and route evidence records `peer_identity_method=advertised_tls_cert_fingerprint_unverified` plus `peer_public_key` when available. The route-evidence API now rejects release-grade identity claims that set `peer_identity_verified=true` without method/key proof material. This remains an unverified material exchange only; release-grade peer identity still requires transport-level key ownership proof and QUIC/TLS encryption on a real second-PC route.

2026-06-01 HTTPS fingerprint-pinned bridge proof: wiki/524, wiki/527, and wiki/528 now distinguish advertised identity material from actual HTTPS certificate proof. Candidate endpoints preserve `scheme`; TLS-enabled bridge URLs advertise `https://`; forwarding to an HTTPS peer with advertised `sha256:<hex>` material uses a fingerprint-pinned rustls client and only records `peer_identity_verified=true`, `peer_identity_method=tls_cert_fingerprint_pin`, and `encryption=https_tls_fingerprint_pin` after the real POST succeeds. The route-evidence API keeps this observable but non-release-grade with `transport_not_release_grade_quic_tls`; final accepted transport remains `quic_tls_1_3`.

Indexer refreshed after HTTPS fingerprint-pinned bridge forwarding, GOAL v120, wiki/524/wiki/527/wiki/528 updates, and CoS memory note `2026-06-01_0735_kst_https_fingerprint_pinned_forwarding.md`: `musu indexer sync --work-dir F:\workspace\musu-bee --name musu-bee` indexed 1076 files and 2096 symbols on 2026-06-01.

2026-06-01 route/relay diagnostic pinning surface: `musu relay status --json` and `musu route --explain --json` now expose `https_fingerprint_pinning_wired=true` plus `release_grade_transport_required=quic_tls_1_3`. Route explain candidate diagnostics can show `transport_scheme`, `peer_identity_method`, `peer_public_key_present`, and `https_fingerprint_pin_available` without converting advertised-only fingerprint material into verified identity. This keeps operator output aligned with the release gate: real evidence must still record `quic_tls_1_3`.

Indexer refreshed after route/relay diagnostic pinning surface, GOAL v121, and CoS memory note `2026-06-01_0757_kst_route_relay_diagnostic_pinning_surface.md`: `musu indexer sync --work-dir F:\workspace\musu-bee --name musu-bee` indexed 1077 files and 2105 symbols on 2026-06-01.

2026-06-01 token-owner scoped route evidence: route evidence storage/query is now scoped by a SHA-256 `owner_key` derived from the accepted Bearer token. `POST /api/v1/p2p/route-evidence` returns `owner_scoped=true`; `GET /api/v1/p2p/route-evidence` filters by the caller's owner key and omits the key from response records. This closes the current shared-bucket stub gap while real account-id mapping, UI/export, and retention policy remain pending.

Indexer refreshed after token-owner scoped route-evidence storage/query, GOAL v122, route-evidence API tests, and CoS memory note `2026-06-01_0815_kst_token_owner_scoped_route_evidence.md`: `musu indexer sync --work-dir F:\workspace\musu-bee --name musu-bee` indexed 1078 files and 2107 symbols on 2026-06-01.

2026-06-01 relay fallback lease policy: `POST /api/v1/p2p/relay/lease` and `GET /api/v1/p2p/relay/lease` now provide the authenticated owner-scoped relay lease boundary. The lease API is fail-closed by default and requires direct route failure, configured relay URL, explicit relay enablement, Connect/Pro-style entitlement, and `MUSU_P2P_RELAY_TRANSPORT_WIRED=1` before issuing a lease. Runtime forwarding now requests a lease after terminal direct-route failure when a rendezvous session/account token exists, but does not relay payload. `musu relay status --json` reports `relay_control_plane_lease_wired=true`, `relay_lease_endpoint=/api/v1/p2p/relay/lease`, `relay_runtime_fallback_lease_request_wired=true`, `relay_default_data_path=false`, and still `relay_transport_wired=false`.

2026-06-01 mDNS/Tailscale log classification: the operator re-supplied the repeated `mdns_sd::service_daemon` Windows `Tailscale` IPv6 multicast failure (`ff02::fb%9:5353`, `os error 10065`, then `closed channel`). 2026-05-31 runtime stabilization execution plan: `MUSU_RUNTIME_STABILIZATION_EXECUTION_PLAN_2026_05_31.md` (wiki/525) locks the execution answer for the three P0 blockers: evidence-first idle CPU profiling, `musu.pro` as P2P control plane and relay policy boundary, and desktop hardening/process ownership as release gates. Process ownership audit now separates MUSU-owned descendants from unrelated machine-wide Node/WebView2 processes and verifies live bridge registry health; startup single-instance audit proves repeated `musu up` reuses the existing bridge PID. Multi-device smoke now emits `musu.route_evidence.v1`; the verifier rejects route evidence without route kind, handshake timing, peer identity verification, hardened encryption, payload transit truth, and success result. This keeps legacy manual HTTP bearer routing useful for debugging but insufficient for public release readiness.

2026-06-01 multi-device verifier hardening: `verify-multidevice-evidence.ps1` now aligns with the `musu.pro` route-evidence API by requiring `peer_identity_method`, `peer_public_key`, and `encryption=quic_tls_1_3` for passing multi-device release evidence. `https_tls_fingerprint_pin` remains useful diagnostic bridge evidence but fails the release verifier with `route encryption release-grade`.

2026-06-01 route evidence transport verifier hardening: `transport_verified_by` is now part of local/cloud route evidence. Release-grade route evidence must set `transport_verified_by=musu_quic_tls_transport`; otherwise `musu.pro` returns `missing_release_grade_transport_proof` and the Windows multi-device verifier fails `route transport proof`. Bridge HTTPS fingerprint-pinned forwarding writes `musu_bridge_forward_fingerprint_pinned_client` through an explicit local `RouteTransportProof`, which remains diagnostic. Rust route evidence treats registry/rendezvous metadata as advertised material only, so even metadata that claims `peer_identity_verified=true`, `quic_tls_1_3`, and `transport_verified_by=musu_quic_tls_transport` is downgraded unless runtime transport code passes local proof.

Source already has the Tauri single-instance plugin, but public release now requires a fresh MSIX build/install plus passing `desktop_single_instance_verified=true` evidence.

2026-06-01 runtime route evidence and mDNS audit: `RUNTIME_ROUTE_EVIDENCE_MDNS_AUDIT_2026_06_01.md` (wiki/528) records the current implementation addendum after the operator supplied Tailscale IPv6 mDNS errors. Route evidence has been promoted from CLI-only helpers into shared `bridge::route_evidence`; `/api/tasks/delegate`, `/api/companies/{id}/run`, and workflow remote steps now write local `musu.route_evidence.v1` files under `~/.musu/route-evidence/` with timing, failure class, rendezvous session id, and advertised peer identity material when present, then start a background best-effort submit of that evidence to `musu.pro` when an account token exists. `musu-bee/src/app/api/v1/p2p/route-evidence/route.ts` is the authenticated route-evidence receive/store/query API; it validates the contract, stores evidence in Vercel KV or an explicit local file fallback, returns `stored=true`, `evidence_id`, `owner_scoped`, `release_grade`, and `blockers`, and supports token-owner scoped filtered `GET` queries. `musu-bee/src/app/api/v1/p2p/rendezvous/*` implements authenticated short-lived session create/read/candidate-update/approve/close endpoints plus recent node candidate cache seeding, and `musu-rs/src/bridge/rendezvous.rs` now wires source/target candidate publish plus target-candidate route selection into bridge forwarding. Relay fallback now has an authenticated owner-scoped lease policy API, and runtime forwarding requests a fail-closed lease after terminal direct-route failure when a rendezvous session/account token exists; relay/tunnel data transport remains unwired. mDNS now default-disables IPv6, Tailscale, and common VPN/virtual interfaces unless `MUSU_MDNS_ENABLE_IPV6=1`, `MUSU_MDNS_ENABLE_TAILSCALE=1`, or `MUSU_MDNS_ENABLE_VIRTUAL_INTERFACES=1` is set. Evidence remains intentionally non-release-grade until transport-verified peer identity, QUIC/TLS encryption proof, real account-id mapping/export, real two-machine proof, and relay/tunnel transport are wired.

2026-05-31 MSIX sideload split update: `audit-msix-desktop-entrypoint.ps1` now records startup contract fields and fails installed audits when the artifact and installed package contracts differ. Local-sideload installed proof `20260531-232229-HUGH_SECOND.local-sideload-installed` passes; Store-reviewed local contract mismatch proof `20260531-232229-HUGH_SECOND.store-reviewed-contract-mismatch` fails as intended because the Store artifact has non-user-configurable startup capability and the local-sideload package does not. The go/no-go desktop-entrypoint gate now requires both Store-reviewed artifact proof and local-sideload installed proof, not a risky local `Add-AppxPackage` of the Store-reviewed restricted-capability package.

## §9 Cross-Reference: Const Gates (per memory `[[feedback-autonomous-loop]]`)

User-gated boundaries (autonomous loop pauses here):
- **Const III** — schema_version / DDL apply on prod databases
- **Const VI** — production deploy (musu.pro, fly.io DNS cutover)
- **Const VII** — main-merge of any branch into `main`/`master`

Per-push Const VII typecheck/test gates are autonomous (no user prompt); main-merge Const VII gate fires only at phase-close bundles (e.g., V23.4 Phase 4 close → wiki/447).

---

## §10 Index Maintenance Notes

- This index is **roll-up only** — when a doc and this index disagree, the doc wins.
- When adding a new wiki/N doc, also append to the correct §1..§5 table here.
- When a `reserved` ID is realized (file created), update Status `reserved → draft → complete`.
- "(wiki/N)" with parens indicates ID was referenced in another doc but the target file lacks an explicit `**Wiki ID**` header — verify before citing externally.
- 2026-06-01 current addendum: wiki/522, wiki/524, wiki/528, and wiki/530 now include the `relay_fallback` route-evidence persistence contract. Search terms should include `relay_fallback`, `lease_requested`, `lease_issued`, `skipped_no_session`, `skipped_no_token`, `relay_lease_denied`, and `stores relay fallback evidence after failed direct route`.
- 2026-06-01 index refresh after that addendum: `musu indexer sync --work-dir F:\workspace\musu-bee --name musu-bee` indexed 1121 files and 2163 symbols.
- 2026-06-01 index refresh after the post-QUIC/TLS-verifier current evidence update: `musu indexer sync --work-dir F:\workspace\musu-bee --name musu-bee` indexed 1130 files and 2163 symbols.
- 2026-06-01 index refresh after route transport-proof hardening and repeated Tailscale IPv6 mDNS log classification: `musu indexer sync --work-dir F:\workspace\musu-bee --name musu-bee` indexed 1131 files and 2165 symbols. Search terms should include `transport_verified_by`, `RouteTransportProof`, `musu_quic_tls_transport`, `missing_release_grade_transport_proof`, `route transport proof`, `musu_bridge_forward_fingerprint_pinned_client`, `ff02::fb%9`, `os error 10065`, and `MUSU_MDNS_ENABLE_TAILSCALE`.
- 2026-06-01 index refresh after runtime CPU scenario matrix gate wiring: `musu indexer sync --work-dir F:\workspace\musu-bee --name musu-bee` indexed 1138 files and 2165 symbols. - 2026-06-27 V34 discovery/stale first bonding:
  `docs/V34_DISCOVERY_STALE_THESIS_2026_06_26.md` now records the first
  candidate-set implementation slices. Bridge cloud heartbeat publishes
  `meta.candidate_endpoints` from the advertised bridge URL plus Tailscale /
  private-mesh IP when present, and now includes every non-virtual usable LAN
  interface candidate via `local_lan_advertise_hosts` /
  `local_candidate_endpoints_for_route_hosts`. Server registry
  `POST /api/v1/nodes/register` adds the request's usable forwarded/source IP
  as `kind: "observed_source_ip"` without replacing `public_url`, and rejects
  loopback/wildcard observed candidates. `peer::discovery` expands cached
  registry candidates into multiple route candidates for the same stable
  `node_name` while rejecting relay/failed/loopback candidates. Remote-usable
  host checks now also reject IPv4-mapped loopback/wildcard hosts such as
  `[::ffff:127.0.0.1]` and `[::ffff:0.0.0.0]` in TS registry write/list and
  Rust resolver/cache paths, and the same rule now covers `musu doctor` /
  `musu nodes` warning helpers plus
  `verify-fleet-audit-contract.ps1 -SelfTestRemoteUsable`. `forward.rs`
  now runs a short read-only `/api/fleet/node-status` preflight over the first
  direct route candidates and moves reachable candidates ahead of stale ones
  before sending a single `/api/tasks/forward` POST. Server registry `listNodes`
  now separates 7-day storage retention from current presence by filtering
  `last_seen` with `MUSU_NODE_REGISTRY_HEARTBEAT_TTL_SEC` /
  `nodeRegistryHeartbeatTtlSeconds`, while `deleteNodeByName` still removes hidden
  stale rows. `src/app/api/health/route.ts` now supplies the production workflow's
  public `GET /api/health` contract (`musu.site_health.v1`) after live
  `https://musu.pro/api/health` returned 404. `verify-musu-pro-install-channel.ps1`
  now includes that health schema/version check, so old production site code cannot
  pass merely because installer URLs return 200. 2026-06-27 production follow-up
  published guarded `desktop-latest` rc.21 assets and deployed Vercel production
  `dpl_E7TrT4SfZm2kEaVvnM4DpW43i9nj`; live `verify-musu-pro-install-channel.ps1 -Json`
  is now `ok=true`, `failure_count=0`, and fleet audit is `warn_count=0`.
  Search terms should include

  and `docs/design-artifacts/pr34-fleet.png`. This is not approval; the remaining
  gate has the design issue URL and artifact URLs, but still requires an explicit
  CEO/design approval comment and `Design: Approved` in the PR body. Search terms should include
  `DESIGN_BRIEF_PR34_FLEET_INSTALL`, `pr34-download.png`, `pr34-install.png`,
  `pr34-fleet.png`, `issue #35`, `approval requested not yet approved`, and
  `Design: Approved`, `fleet-proof command on install pages`, and
  `release-grade JSON evidence`.

- 2026-06-27 product readiness code audit:
  `docs/MUSU_PRODUCT_READINESS_CODE_AUDIT_2026_06_27.md` records the current
  purpose-aligned code audit after the pasted runtime findings. The code-level
  false-freshness bugs are fixed: registry `last_seen` is no longer replaced by
  fetch time, loopback/wildcard/port-0 `public_url` values are rejected, unusable
  cached registry rows do not suppress valid peers, and relay-display is not
  counted in `online_nodes`. The audit also records the public install-page
  follow-up: `/download` and `/install` now expose `fleet-proof.ps1`, with a
  public metadata contract test keeping the command visible. The audit now records
  physical `hugh-main` `fleet-proof.ps1` JSON saved under
  `docs/evidence/fleet-proof/1.15.0-rc.22/hugh-main-20260627T010201Z.fleet-proof.json`;
  current rc.22 two-PC direct readiness is green, and the remaining blocker is
  real PR #34 design approval. Search
  terms should include `MUSU_PRODUCT_READINESS_CODE_AUDIT`,
  `false-online fixes`, `registry_last_seen_to_heartbeat`,
  `online_nodes_direct_only`, `hugh-main proof green`,
  `issue #35 approval missing`, `fleet-proof.ps1 public install pages`,
  `hugh-main-20260627T010201Z.fleet-proof.json`, and
  `next action packet`.

- 2026-06-27 hugh-main hosted fleet proof accepted:
  Physical main PC proof is now saved at
  `docs/evidence/fleet-proof/1.15.0-rc.22/hugh-main-20260627T010201Z.fleet-proof.json`.
  It was generated by
  `& ([scriptblock]::Create((irm https://musu.pro/fleet-proof.ps1))) -ExpectedNodeName hugh-main -ExpectedDirectPeerName hugh_second -RequireBrainToken -Json`
  and returned `schema=musu.fleet_node_proof.v1`, `ok=true`, `fail_count=0`,
  `warn_count=0`, `installed_package_version=1.15.0.22`,
  `package_full_name=blossompark.musu_1.15.0.22_x64__f5h38pf4yt4gc`,
  `bridge_bind_addr=0.0.0.0:4387`, `advertised_public_url=http://192.168.1.192:4387`,
  `online_nodes=2`, `direct_healthy_nodes=2`, `remote_cloud_warning_count=0`,
  expected direct peer `hugh_second`, and `brain_ingest_token_acl_restricted`.
  Follow-up `musu status --json` from `hugh_second` also showed both
  `hugh_second` and `hugh-main` healthy via direct routes. This closes the
  rc.22 two-physical-machine direct proof blocker; PR #34 design approval,
  Store readiness, and real relay transport remain separate unproven claims.
  The same status was propagated into
  `docs/RELEASE_1_15_0_RC22_INSTALL_CHANNEL_AUDIT_NEXT_STEPS_2026_06_27.md`,

  text no longer says `hugh-main` physical proof is missing.
  Indexer refresh after this proof/doc sync:

  3313 files and 3847 symbols. Recall query

  release next steps, evidence JSON, readiness audit, V34 thesis, and handoff.

- 2026-06-27 design-gate token hardening:
  `scripts/design-gate/evaluate.cjs` now accepts `Design: Approved` only as a
  standalone status line. This fixes the PR-body bypass where a pending PR could
  mention `` `Design: Approved` `` inside an instruction and make design-gate
  pass. Regression coverage lives in `scripts/design-gate/evaluate.test.cjs`,
  and `.github/workflows/design-gate.yml` now runs
  `node --test scripts/design-gate/*.test.cjs` before PR evidence evaluation.
  Search terms should include `standalone status line`, `Design: Pending`,
  `Design: Approved instruction bypass`, `design-gate token hardening`, and
  `Run design-gate evaluator tests`.

- 2026-06-27 full product spec completion roadmap:
  `docs/MUSU_FULL_PRODUCT_SPEC_COMPLETION_ROADMAP_2026_06_27.md` is the
  canonical answer to whether MUSU is fully complete against the whole product
  spec. Current answer: no, not yet. `1.15.0-rc.22` proves the two-PC direct
  fleet slice on `hugh-main` and `hugh_second`, but full product completion
  still requires PR #34 design approval, Store or trusted distribution evidence,
  real delegated-work relay transport, full brain health/task-ingest/UX proof,
  V34 stale self-heal proof, and either support mailbox evidence or a formal
  retirement of that historical gate. `PRODUCT_PURPOSE_AND_IMPLEMENTATION_GATE`
  now points to this roadmap and scopes the current claim to rc.22 direct fleet
  readiness. Search terms should include
  `MUSU_FULL_PRODUCT_SPEC_COMPLETION_ROADMAP`, `full product not complete`,
  `two-PC direct fleet slice`, `relay transport not complete`,
  `brain product proof`, `Store trusted distribution evidence`,
  `V34 stale self-heal`, and `support mailbox retire gate`.
